    ("Tactics.system_responds_action_caseE",
     "[| (\<lbrace>?l\<rbrace> Response ?action, ?afts)
         : fragments (gc_coms ?p) {};
         ?v : ?action (?pname, ?req) ?s;
         [| ?p = sys;
            case ?req of
            ro_MFENCE =>
              ?l = sys.tso_mfence &
              ?action =
              (%req s.
                  {uu_.
                   uu_ = (s, mv_Void) &
                   (EX p. req = (p, ro_MFENCE) &
                          mem_store_buffers s p = [])}) &
              ?afts =
              lconst
               {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut, sys.sys_hs_mut_pending,
                sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W, sys.sys_hs_gc_done,
                sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs, sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type,
                sys.sys_free, Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc,
                sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer, sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock,
                sys.tso_mfence, sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
              ?v = (?s, mv_Void) & mem_store_buffers ?s ?pname = []
            | ro_Load x2 =>
                ?l = sys.tso_load &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {(s, sys_load p mr s) |p mr.
                     req = (p, ro_Load mr) & not_blocked s p}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                (EX p mr.
                    ?v = (?s, sys_load p mr ?s) &
                    (?pname = p & x2 = mr) & not_blocked ?s p)
            | ro_Store x3 =>
                ?l = sys.tso_store &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {(s(| mem_store_buffers := (mem_store_buffers s)
                            (p := mem_store_buffers s p @ [w]) |),
                      mv_Void) |
                     p w. req = (p, ro_Store w)}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                (EX p w.
                    ?v =
                    (?s(| mem_store_buffers := (mem_store_buffers ?s)
                            (p := mem_store_buffers ?s p @ [w]) |),
                     mv_Void) &
                    ?pname = p & x3 = w)
            | ro_Lock =>
                ?l = sys.tso_lock &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {(s(| mem_lock := Some p |), mv_Void) |p.
                     req = (p, ro_Lock) & mem_lock s = None}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                (EX p. ?v = (?s(| mem_lock := Some p |), mv_Void) &
                       ?pname = p & mem_lock ?s = None)
            | ro_Unlock =>
                ?l = sys.tso_unlock &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {uu_.
                     uu_ = (mem_lock_update Map.empty s, mv_Void) &
                     (EX p. req = (p, ro_Unlock) &
                            mem_lock s = Some p &
                            mem_store_buffers s p = [])}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                ?v = (mem_lock_update Map.empty ?s, mv_Void) &
                mem_lock ?s = Some ?pname & mem_store_buffers ?s ?pname = []
            | ro_Alloc =>
                ?l = Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    if {a. EX y. local_state.heap s a = Some y} = UNIV
                    then {uu_. uu_ = (s, mv_Ref None) & snd req = ro_Alloc}
                    else {(s(| heap := local_state.heap s(r |->
                                 (| obj_mark = fA s, obj_fields = Map.empty,
                                    obj_payload = Map.empty |)) |),
                           mv_Ref (Some r)) |
                          r. r ~: dom (local_state.heap s) &
                             snd req = ro_Alloc}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                ?v : (if {a. EX y. local_state.heap ?s a = Some y} = UNIV
                      then {uu_. uu_ = (?s, mv_Ref None)}
                      else {(?s(| heap := local_state.heap ?s(r |->
                                    (| obj_mark = fA ?s,
 obj_fields = Map.empty, obj_payload = Map.empty |)) |),
                             mv_Ref (Some r)) |
                            r. r ~: dom (local_state.heap ?s)})
            | ro_Free x7 =>
                ?l = sys.sys_free &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {(s(| heap := (local_state.heap s)(r := None) |),
                      mv_Void) |
                     r. snd req = ro_Free r}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                (EX r. ?v =
                       (?s(| heap := (local_state.heap ?s)(r := None) |),
                        mv_Void) &
                       x7 = r)
            | ro_hs_gc_load_pending x8 =>
                ?l = sys.sys_hs_gc_done &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {(s, mv_Bool (~ hs_pending s m)) |m.
                     req = (gc, ro_hs_gc_load_pending m)}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                (EX m. ?v = (?s, mv_Bool (~ hs_pending ?s m)) &
                       ?pname = gc & x8 = m)
            | ro_hs_gc_store_type x9 =>
                ?l = sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {(s(| hs_type := ht, ghost_hs_in_sync := %s. False,
                          ghost_hs_phase :=
                            hp_step ht (ghost_hs_phase s) |),
                      mv_Void) |
                     ht. req = (gc, ro_hs_gc_store_type ht)}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                (EX ht.
                    ?v =
                    (?s(| hs_type := ht, ghost_hs_in_sync := %s. False,
                          ghost_hs_phase :=
                            hp_step ht (ghost_hs_phase ?s) |),
                     mv_Void) &
                    ?pname = gc & x9 = ht)
            | ro_hs_gc_store_pending x10 =>
                ?l = sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {(s(| hs_pending := (hs_pending s)(m := True) |),
                      mv_Void) |
                     m. req = (gc, ro_hs_gc_store_pending m)}) &

                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,

                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                (EX m. ?v =
                       (?s(| hs_pending := (hs_pending ?s)(m := True) |),
                        mv_Void) &
                       ?pname = gc & x10 = m)
            | ro_hs_gc_load_W =>
                ?l = sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W &
                ?action =

                    {uu_.
                     uu_ = (s(| W := {} |), mv_Refs (W s)) &
                     req = (gc, ro_hs_gc_load_W)}) &

    ("Tactics.system_responds_action_specE",
     "[| (\<lbrace>?l\<rbrace> Response ?action, ?afts)
         : fragments (gc_coms ?p) {};
         ?v : ?action ?x ?s;
         [| ?p = sys;
            case snd ?x of
            ro_MFENCE =>
              ?l = sys.tso_mfence &
              ?action =
              (%req s.
                  {uu_.
                   uu_ = (s, mv_Void) &
                   (EX p. req = (p, ro_MFENCE) &
                          mem_store_buffers s p = [])}) &
              ?afts =
              lconst
               {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut, sys.sys_hs_mut_pending,
                sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W, sys.sys_hs_gc_done,
                sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs, sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type,
                sys.sys_free, Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc,
                sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer, sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock,
                sys.tso_mfence, sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
              ?v = (?s, mv_Void) & mem_store_buffers ?s (fst ?x) = []
            | ro_Load x2 =>
                ?l = sys.tso_load &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {(s, sys_load p mr s) |p mr.
                     req = (p, ro_Load mr) & not_blocked s p}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                (EX p mr.
                    ?v = (?s, sys_load p mr ?s) &
                    (fst ?x = p & x2 = mr) & not_blocked ?s p)
            | ro_Store x3 =>
                ?l = sys.tso_store &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {(s(| mem_store_buffers := (mem_store_buffers s)
                            (p := mem_store_buffers s p @ [w]) |),
                      mv_Void) |
                     p w. req = (p, ro_Store w)}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                (EX p w.
                    ?v =
                    (?s(| mem_store_buffers := (mem_store_buffers ?s)
                            (p := mem_store_buffers ?s p @ [w]) |),
                     mv_Void) &
                    fst ?x = p & x3 = w)
            | ro_Lock =>
                ?l = sys.tso_lock &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {(s(| mem_lock := Some p |), mv_Void) |p.
                     req = (p, ro_Lock) & mem_lock s = None}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                (EX p. ?v = (?s(| mem_lock := Some p |), mv_Void) &
                       fst ?x = p & mem_lock ?s = None)
            | ro_Unlock =>
                ?l = sys.tso_unlock &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {uu_.
                     uu_ = (mem_lock_update Map.empty s, mv_Void) &
                     (EX p. req = (p, ro_Unlock) &
                            mem_lock s = Some p &
                            mem_store_buffers s p = [])}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                ?v = (mem_lock_update Map.empty ?s, mv_Void) &
                mem_lock ?s = Some (fst ?x) &
                mem_store_buffers ?s (fst ?x) = []
            | ro_Alloc =>
                ?l = Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    if {a. EX y. local_state.heap s a = Some y} = UNIV
                    then {uu_. uu_ = (s, mv_Ref None) & snd req = ro_Alloc}
                    else {(s(| heap := local_state.heap s(r |->
                                 (| obj_mark = fA s, obj_fields = Map.empty,
                                    obj_payload = Map.empty |)) |),
                           mv_Ref (Some r)) |
                          r. r ~: dom (local_state.heap s) &
                             snd req = ro_Alloc}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                ?v : (if {a. EX y. local_state.heap ?s a = Some y} = UNIV
                      then {uu_. uu_ = (?s, mv_Ref None)}
                      else {(?s(| heap := local_state.heap ?s(r |->
                                    (| obj_mark = fA ?s,
 obj_fields = Map.empty, obj_payload = Map.empty |)) |),
                             mv_Ref (Some r)) |
                            r. r ~: dom (local_state.heap ?s)})
            | ro_Free x7 =>
                ?l = sys.sys_free &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {(s(| heap := (local_state.heap s)(r := None) |),
                      mv_Void) |
                     r. snd req = ro_Free r}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                (EX r. ?v =
                       (?s(| heap := (local_state.heap ?s)(r := None) |),
                        mv_Void) &
                       x7 = r)
            | ro_hs_gc_load_pending x8 =>
                ?l = sys.sys_hs_gc_done &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {(s, mv_Bool (~ hs_pending s m)) |m.
                     req = (gc, ro_hs_gc_load_pending m)}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                (EX m. ?v = (?s, mv_Bool (~ hs_pending ?s m)) &
                       fst ?x = gc & x8 = m)
            | ro_hs_gc_store_type x9 =>
                ?l = sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {(s(| hs_type := ht, ghost_hs_in_sync := %s. False,
                          ghost_hs_phase :=
                            hp_step ht (ghost_hs_phase s) |),
                      mv_Void) |
                     ht. req = (gc, ro_hs_gc_store_type ht)}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                (EX ht.
                    ?v =
                    (?s(| hs_type := ht, ghost_hs_in_sync := %s. False,
                          ghost_hs_phase :=
                            hp_step ht (ghost_hs_phase ?s) |),
                     mv_Void) &
                    fst ?x = gc & x9 = ht)
            | ro_hs_gc_store_pending x10 =>
                ?l = sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {(s(| hs_pending := (hs_pending s)(m := True) |),
                      mv_Void) |
                     m. req = (gc, ro_hs_gc_store_pending m)}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                (EX m. ?v =
                       (?s(| hs_pending := (hs_pending ?s)(m := True) |),
                        mv_Void) &
                       fst ?x = gc & x10 = m)
            | ro_hs_gc_load_W =>
                ?l = sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {uu_.
                     uu_ = (s(| W := {} |), mv_Refs (W s)) &
                     req = (gc, ro_hs_gc_load_W)}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                ?v = (?s(| W := {} |), mv_Refs (W ?s)) & fst ?x = gc
            | ro_hs_mut_load_pending =>
                ?l = sys.sys_hs_mut_pending &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {(s, mv_Bool (hs_pending s m)) |m.
                     req = (mutator m, ro_hs_mut_load_pending)}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                (EX m. ?v = (?s, mv_Bool (hs_pending ?s m)) &
                       fst ?x = mutator m)
            | ro_hs_mut_load_type =>
                ?l = sys.sys_hs_mut &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {uu_.
                     uu_ = (s, mv_hs_type (hs_type s)) &
                     (EX m. req = (mutator m, ro_hs_mut_load_type))}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                ?v = (?s, mv_hs_type (hs_type ?s)) &
                (EX m. fst ?x = mutator m)
            | ro_hs_mut_done x14 =>
                ?l = sys.sys_hs_mut_done &
                ?action =
                (%req s.
                    {(s(| hs_pending := (hs_pending s)(m := False),
                          W := W s Un W',
                          ghost_hs_in_sync := (ghost_hs_in_sync s)
                            (m := True) |),
                      mv_Void) |
                     m W'. req = (mutator m, ro_hs_mut_done W')}) &
                ?afts =
                lconst
                 {sys.sys_hs_mut_done, sys.sys_hs_mut,
                  sys.sys_hs_mut_pending, sys.sys_hs_gc_load_W,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_done, sys.sys_hs_gc_mut_reqs,
                  sys.sys_hs_gc_set_type, sys.sys_free,
                  Proofs_Basis.sys.alloc, sys.tso_dequeue_store_buffer,
                  sys.tso_unlock, sys.tso_lock, sys.tso_mfence,
                  sys.tso_store, sys.tso_load} &
                (EX m W'.
                    ?v =
                    (?s(| hs_pending := (hs_pending ?s)(m := False),
                          W := W ?s Un W',
                          ghost_hs_in_sync := (ghost_hs_in_sync ?s)
                            (m := True) |),
                     mv_Void) &
                    fst ?x = mutator m & x14 = W') |]
         ==> ?Q |]
      ==> ?Q",
